    (function() {
         var ft;
         var delta;
         var q = [];
         function processQueue() {
             var now = new Date();
             for (var i=0; i < q.length; i++) {
                 var delay = now - q[i].time;
                 console.warn('delay of ' + delay + 'ms due to time fetching.');
                 q[i].callback(ft, delta);
             }
             q.length = 0;
         }
         function fetchTimeFromAkamai() {
             var req = new XMLHttpRequest();
             req.addEventListener("error", function l() {
                 console.warn('time fetching error.');
                 ft = new Date();
                 delta = 0;
                 processQueue();
             });
             req.addEventListener("timeout", function l() {
                 console.warn('time fetching timed out.');
                 ft = new Date();
                 delta = 0;
                 processQueue();
             });
             req.addEventListener("load", function l(x, y) {
                 if (req.status === 200) {
                     ft = new Date(this.responseText);
                     delta = ft - new Date();
                 } else {
                     console.warn('time fetching failed.');
                     ft = new Date();
                     delta = 0;
                 }
                 processQueue();
             });
             req.open("GET", "//time.akamai.com/?iso");
             req.timeout = 1000;
             req.send();
         }
         window.onAkamaiTimeReference = function(callback) {
             if (ft) {
                 callback(ft, delta);
             } else {
                 q.push({ callback: callback, time: new Date() });
             }
         }
         fetchTimeFromAkamai();
     })();
